FROM [Reports] AS [r]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[SampleName]
    FROM [Samples] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t] ON [r].[SampleId] = [t].[Id]

    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[UserId]
    FROM [Employees] AS [e]
    WHERE [e].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [r].[EmployeeId] = [t0].[Id]
